 ' gadakari ne is silsile main ek vakya bayaan kiya ki kaise unke apane pie ne ek railway stesan master ko nirdesh diya ki gadakari jis train main safar kar rahe hai, vah nikaas maarg se lage plateform number-1 par ruke

 i kept wondering because it was done without my knowledge

 5 megahatrj se atirikt spectrum ke liye bhugtan karenge
 Chidambaram said that the dot will submit the pricing format to the CDMA operators to the Cabinet, as there is no operator present to bid in the CDMA auction, so the auction will not determine the price
 tata teleservices or videokon ke spectrum nilaamee se baahar ho jane ke baad ab sidime kii nilaamee main boli lagane vaala koi nahin bachaa
 6
 2 megahatrj se adhik spectrum rakhane vaale sanchaalak july 2008 se lagu hone vaali keemat kaa bhugtan karenge
 Operators with a maximum of 4
 4 megahertz spectrum hi he, unase koi shulk nahin liya jayega
 The comments mantrimandal ne sanchaalkon ko spectrum saajha karne kii anumati dene kii mantristareey samiti kii sifarish ko bhi manjuuri de di
 The cabinet also decided to end the provision for imposing additional charges on mergers and acquisitions in the telecom sector

 ve
 Kanoria said, "obama's historic second term bodes well for the newly established indo-us economic and strategic relationship
 " Obama defeated Republican candidate Mitt Romney on Tuesday
 obama ke phir se raashtrapati chune jane se fikki ne kaha ki isse bharat-america aarthik rishta aage badhegaa lekin bharat ke liye ek maatr chintaa kii baat obama kii outsorcig chintaa he
 Kanoria said, "I think the indo-us strategic and business and economic relationship will definitely continue beyond their re-election
" " In the election campaign, however, Obama criticized outsourcing of jobs to countries like India and said that America needs to create jobs locally
 canoria ne kaha, "chintaa kii ek maatr baat outsorcing par unki soch he
 i believe that there is a misconception that outsourcing to India will reduce jobs in the US
 anek adhyayanon se pataa chal chukaa he ki aisa nahin hoga

 Approved lump sum fee for companies holding 2G spectrum over 4 mhz
 yah shulk utana hi hoga, jitna agle saptaah hone vaali nilaamee main saamne aayega
 This fee was recommended by the Empowered Group of Ministers to present equality of opportunity for new and old players in the market
 mantrimandal kii baithak ke baad vitt mantri pi
 Chidambaram said that the GSM operators should have 4
 4 megahatrj se adhik spectrum ke liye bhugtan karne ke liye kaha jayega or isaki keemat 12 navambar se shuru hone vaali nilaamee se nirdhaarit hogi
 2 for the remaining period of the CDMA Operator's Permit
 5 megahatrj se atirikt spectrum ke liye bhugtan karenge
 Chidambaram said that the dot will submit the pricing format to the CDMA operators to the Cabinet, as there is no operator present to bid in the CDMA auction, so the auction will not determine the price

 federation of indian chambers of commers and industry (fikki) ke adhyaksh aar
 V
 canoria ne kaha, "obama kaa aitihaasik doosraa kaarykaal nav sthapit bharat-america aarthik tathaa ranneetik sambandh ke liye shubh sanket he
 " obama ne mangalvaar ko republican ummidavaar mit romany ko parajeet kiya
 After Obama was re-elected President, FICCI said that this will increase the india-us economic relationship but the only concern for India is Obama's outsourcing concern
 canoria ne kaha, "mere khyal se bharat-america ranneetik or kaarobaari tathaa aarthik rishta unke punarnirvachan se nishchit rup se aage jari rahegaa
 " chunaav abhiyaan main haalanki obama ne bharat jaise deshon ko naukariyon kii outsorcig kii aalochana kii thi or kaha tha ki america ko sthaneey str par naukari kaa srijan karne kii jarurat he
 Kanoria said, "the only thing of concern is his thinking on outsourcing
 meraa maananaa he ki yah galat dharna he ki bharat ko outsorcing se america main naukari ghategi
 Many studies have shown that this will not happen
 " The Union Cabinet on Thursday 4
 4 megahatrj se adhik 2ji spectrum rakhane vaali companiyon ke liye ekamusth shulk ko manjuuri de di
 This fee will be the same as that seen in the auction next week
 bazaar ke nae or puraane khilaadiyon ke liye avasar kii samanta prastut karne ke liye mantriyon ke adhikaar praapt samooh ne is shulk kii sifarish kii thi
 Finance Minister P
 after the cabinet meeting
 chidambaram ne kaha ki jiesem sanchaalkon ko 4
 For spectrum over 4 mhz will be asked to pay and its price will be determined from the auction starting November 12
 sidime sanchaalak permit kii bachi hui avadhi ke liye 2
 Will pay for additional spectrum from 5 mhz
 chidambaram ne kaha ki doorsanchaar vibhaag sidime sanchaalkon ke liye mulya nirdhaaran kaa praaroop mantrimandal ko prastut karegaa, kyonki sidime kii nilaamee main boli lagane ke liye koi sanchaalak maujuud nahin he isliye nilaamee se mulya nirdhaarit nahin ho paaegaa
 After Tata Teleservices and Videocon went out of the spectrum auction, there was no bidder left in the CDMA auction
 6
 Operators with spectrum above 2 mhz will pay the applicable price from July 2008
 jin sanchaalkon ke paas adhiktam 4
 There is only 4 mhz spectrum, they will not be charged
 tippaniyan The Cabinet also approved the recommendation of the Ministerial Committee to allow operators to share spectrum
 mantrimandal ne doorsanchaar kshetra main vilay or adhigrahan par atirikt shulk lagane ke pravadhan ko bhi samaapt karne kaa faisla kiya

 world aids vaxin de prativarsh 18 may ko manaaya jaataa he
 This day is celebrated with the aim of making people aware of AIDS
 ise echivi vaxin awarenes de bhi kaha jaataa he
 The day was first celebrated on 18 May 1997
 aaie world aids vaxin de ke maukey par jaanate hai aakhir yah failata kaise or isse bachaav ke tareeke kya hai?aids ko equared immuno defishiency syndrome ke rup main bhi janaa jaataa he
 HIV means a human immunodeficiency virus
 yah vyakti kii pratiraksha pranali ko kamjor banaakar uske rakt ko safed pani main badal detaa he
 How to spread AIDS In the event of sexual intercourse with someone without protection, chances of spreading AIDS are very high
 ek hi syringe or sui kaa istemaal agar baar-baar kiya jaae to isse bhi sankraman failane kaa khatra kaaphi bad jaataa he
 It can also be spread by using hiv-infected blood-contaminated needles or medical devices on someone else
 sankramit yoni srav, veery or khule ghaavon ke sampark main aane se bhi beemaari fail sakati he
 It can also happen by breastfeeding an infected woman's baby
 kya hai aids se bachaav ke tareekesharir main virus ke zyada haaavee hone ke ise control karnaa kaaphi mushkil ha jota he
 Anti-retroviral therapies and medicines are used in the treatment of AIDS
 in dawaaiyon kaa mukhya uddeshy echivi ke prabhaav ko kaam karnaa, sharir kii rog pratirohak kshamta ko majboot karnaa or avasarwaadi rogon ko thik karnaa hota he

 9

 11

 12

 India today successfully launched its first space observatory 'astrosat' based on the goal of developing a detailed understanding of the universe
 pieselvi-si30 ke jariye sriharikota se prakshepit kiya gaya estrosat apane saath chah videshi upgrah bhi le gaya he, jinamein se chaar america upgrah hai
 This is the first time India has launched US satellites
 ye upgrah san francisco kii ek company ke hai
 These have been launched under an agreement with Antrix Corporation Limited, the commercial arm of the Indian Space Research Organization (ISRO)
 satish dhawan antariksh centre se kiye gaye is prakshepan main isro ke vishwasaneey polar satellite launch whical (pieselvi) kii madad lee gai
 As part of its 31st flight, PSLV placed the astrosat and its six co-passengers (satellites) into orbit approximately 25 minutes after the flight began

 The Astrosat campaign has a duration of five years and has four X-ray payloads, an ultraviolet telescope and a charge particle monitor
 kai khaas visheshthaenvaigyanik upgrah abhiyaan estrosat main kai khaas visheshtaayen bhi hai
 As such, it can collect data of waves of different lengths associated with different celestial bodies through a single satellite
 isro ke anusaar, estrosat brahmad kaa adhyayan vidyutchumbakeey spectrum ke prakaashiya, parabangnee or ucch urja vaali eksre ke kshetron main karegaa jabaki adhiktar anya vaigyanik upgrah vibhinn lambaai kii tarangon ke ek sankeern failaav (nairo range) kaa hi adhyayan karne main sakasham hote hai
 During the entire period of operation of the satellite, it will be managed by the spacecraft control center at the Mission Operations Complex of ISRO Telemetry, Tracking and Command Network, Bangalore
 estrosat ke vaigyanik uddeshy neutron stars or blike hole se yukt binary star system (do taron kaa samooh) kii ucch urja prakriyaaon kaa adhyayan karnaa, neutron stars ke chumbakeey kshetra kaa akalan or taron ke janm kshetron evam hamaari akashganga se pare maujuud taramandalon kii ucch urja prakriyaaon kaa adhyayan karnaa he
 The mission aims to identify new less bright x-ray sources in the sky and to conduct a limited deep field survey of the universe in the ultraviolet region
